(* This file is the first file with the purpose of showing that any monoidal category admits a 'Monoidal Rezk-completion'.
More precisely: Assume that a category C is weakly equivalent to a univalent category D, by a functor H : C → D.
Then, given a product/tensor T : C ⊠ C → C, we construct a product TD on D such that H preserves the product in a 'strong sense'.
Then, we show that (D,TD) is universal along univalent categories with a product in the sense that
(D,TD) is the free univalent category equipped with a tensor of (C,T).
A more detailled explanation of the universality and the Rezk-completion is in LiftedMonoidal.v
*)

Require Import UniMath.Foundations.All.

Local Open Scope mor_disp.
Local Open Scope cat.

Section TensorRezk.

  Context {C D E : category} {H : functor C D}
          (Duniv : is_univalent D)
          (Euniv : is_univalent E)
          (H_eso : essentially_surjective H)
          (H_ff : fully_faithful H).

  Context (TC : functor (C ⊠ C) C)
          (TE : functor (E ⊠ E) E).

  Local Notation HH := (pair_functor H H).
  Let HH_eso := pair_functor_eso H H H_eso H_eso.
  Let HH_ff := pair_functor_ff H H H_ff H_ff.

  Definition TransportedTensor
    : functor (D ⊠ D) D
    := lift_functor_along (_,,Duniv) HH HH_eso HH_ff (functor_composite TC H).

  Definition TransportedTensorComm
    : nat_z_iso (HH ∙ TransportedTensor)
                (functor_composite TC H)
    := lift_functor_along_comm (_,,Duniv) HH HH_eso HH_ff (functor_composite TC H).

  Let TD := TransportedTensor.

  
C, D, E: category
H: C ⟶ D
Duniv: is_univalent D
Euniv: is_univalent E
H_eso: essentially_surjective H
H_ff: fully_faithful H
TC: C ⊠ C ⟶ C
TE: E ⊠ E ⟶ E
HH_eso:= pair_functor_eso H H H_eso H_eso: essentially_surjective HH
HH_ff:= pair_functor_ff H H H_ff H_ff: fully_faithful HH
TD:= TransportedTensor: D ⊠ D ⟶ D
disp_functor_data (pre_composition_functor C D E H)
  (functor_tensor_disp_cat TD TE)
  (functor_tensor_disp_cat TC TE)

∏ (x y : [D, E])
(xx : functor_tensor_disp_cat TD TE x)
(yy : functor_tensor_disp_cat TD TE y)
(f : [D, E] ⟦ x, y ⟧),
xx -->[ f] yy
→ functor_tensor_composition
    (pr1 TransportedTensorComm) xx -->[
  # (pre_composition_functor C D E H) f] functor_tensor_composition
                                           (pr1
                                              TransportedTensorComm)
                                           yy

GG2: functor_tensor_disp_cat TD TE G2

ββ: GG1 -->[ β] GG2
functor_tensor_composition (pr1 TransportedTensorComm)
  GG1 -->[

                                         (pr1
                                            TransportedTensorComm)
                                         GG2

x, y: C
# TE
  (# (pre_composition_functor C D E H) β x
  #, # (pre_composition_functor C D E H) β y)
· functor_tensor_composition
    (pr1 TransportedTensorComm) GG2 (x, y) =
functor_tensor_composition (pr1 TransportedTensorComm)
  GG1 (x, y)
· # (pre_composition_functor C D E H) β (TC (x, y))

   · # G2
       (rad_eps [precategory_binproduct_data D D, D]
          [precategory_binproduct_data C C, D]

GG1 (H x, H y)
· # G1
    (rad_eps [precategory_binproduct_data D D, D]

       [precategory_binproduct_data C C, D]
       (pre_composition_functor (C ⊠ C) (D ⊠ D) D HH)
       (ff_essentially_surjective_to_split
          [precategory_binproduct_data D D, D]
          [precategory_binproduct_data C C, D]
          (is_univalent_functor_category
             (precategory_binproduct_data D D) D Duniv)
          (pre_composition_functor (C ⊠ C) (D ⊠ D) D
             HH)
          (precomp_fully_faithful.pre_composition_with_ess_surj_and_fully_faithful_is_fully_faithful
             (C ⊠ C) (D ⊠ D) D HH HH_eso HH_ff)
          (precomp_ess_surj.pre_composition_essentially_surjective
             (C ⊠ C) (D ⊠ D) D Duniv HH HH_eso HH_ff))
       (TC ∙ H) (x, y)) =
# G1
  (rad_eps [precategory_binproduct_data D D, D]
     [precategory_binproduct_data C C, D]
     (pre_composition_functor (C ⊠ C) (D ⊠ D) D HH)
     (ff_essentially_surjective_to_split
        [precategory_binproduct_data D D, D]
        [precategory_binproduct_data C C, D]
        (is_univalent_functor_category
           (precategory_binproduct_data D D) D Duniv)
        (pre_composition_functor (C ⊠ C) (D ⊠ D) D HH)
        (precomp_fully_faithful.pre_composition_with_ess_surj_and_fully_faithful_is_fully_faithful
           (C ⊠ C) (D ⊠ D) D HH HH_eso HH_ff)
        (precomp_ess_surj.pre_composition_essentially_surjective
           (C ⊠ C) (D ⊠ D) D Duniv HH HH_eso HH_ff))
     (TC ∙ H) (x, y)) · pr1 β (pr1 H (TC (x, y)))

    exact (! pr2 β _ _ (pr1 (pr1 (TransportedTensorComm)) (x, y))).
  Defined.

H: C ⟶ D
Duniv: is_univalent D
Euniv: is_univalent E
H_eso: essentially_surjective H
H_ff: fully_faithful H
TC: C ⊠ C ⟶ C

HGG: functor_tensor_disp_cat TC TE
  (pre_composition_functor C D E H G)
c1, c2: C
β:= nat_trans_comp
  (functor_tensor_map_dom TE (functor_compose H G))
  (functor_tensor_map_codom TC
     (functor_compose H G))
  (HH ∙ functor_tensor_map_codom TD G) HGG
  (post_whisker
     (nat_z_iso_inv TransportedTensorComm) G)
:
HH ∙ (pair_functor G G ∙ TE)
⟹ HH ∙ functor_tensor_map_codom TD G: HH ∙ (pair_functor G G ∙ TE)
⟹ HH ∙ functor_tensor_map_codom TD G
HGG (c1, c2) =
lifted_functor_tensor HGG (H c1, H c2)
· # G
    (rad_eps [precategory_binproduct_data D D, D]
       [precategory_binproduct_data C C, D]
       (pre_composition_functor (C ⊠ C) (D ⊠ D) D HH)

             HH)

             (C ⊠ C) (D ⊠ D) D HH HH_eso HH_ff)

C, D, E: category
H: C ⟶ D
Duniv: is_univalent D
Euniv: is_univalent E
H_eso: essentially_surjective H
H_ff: fully_faithful H
TC: C ⊠ C ⟶ C
TE: E ⊠ E ⟶ E
HH_eso:= pair_functor_eso H H H_eso H_eso: essentially_surjective HH
HH_ff:= pair_functor_ff H H H_ff H_ff: fully_faithful HH
TD:= TransportedTensor: D ⊠ D ⟶ D
G: [D, E]
HGG: functor_tensor_disp_cat TC TE
  (pre_composition_functor C D E H G)
c1, c2: C
β:= nat_trans_comp
  (functor_tensor_map_dom TE (functor_compose H G))
  (functor_tensor_map_codom TC
     (functor_compose H G))
  (HH ∙ functor_tensor_map_codom TD G) HGG
  (post_whisker
     (nat_z_iso_inv TransportedTensorComm) G)
:
HH ∙ (pair_functor G G ∙ TE)
⟹ HH ∙ functor_tensor_map_codom TD G: HH ∙ (pair_functor G G ∙ TE)
⟹ HH ∙ functor_tensor_map_codom TD G
p:= toforallpaths
  (λ x : C ⊠ C,
   (E,, Euniv)
   ⟦ functor_composite_data HH
       (pair_functor G G ∙ TE) x,
   functor_composite_data HH
     (functor_tensor_map_codom TD G) x ⟧)
  (pr1
     (pre_whisker HH
        (lift_nat_trans_along 
           (E,, Euniv) HH HH_eso HH_ff β))) 
  (pr1 β)
  (base_paths
     (pre_whisker HH
        (lift_nat_trans_along 
           (E,, Euniv) HH HH_eso HH_ff β)) β
     (lift_nat_trans_along_comm 
        (E,, Euniv) HH HH_eso HH_ff β)) 
  (c1, c2): pr1
  (pre_whisker HH
     (lift_nat_trans_along 
        (E,, Euniv) HH HH_eso HH_ff β)) 
  (c1, c2) = pr1 β (c1, c2)
HGG (c1, c2) =
lifted_functor_tensor HGG (H c1, H c2)
· # G
    (rad_eps [precategory_binproduct_data D D, D]
       [precategory_binproduct_data C C, D]
       (pre_composition_functor (C ⊠ C) (D ⊠ D) D HH)
       (ff_essentially_surjective_to_split
          [precategory_binproduct_data D D, D]

             (precategory_binproduct_data D D) D Duniv)

             HH)

             (C ⊠ C) (D ⊠ D) D HH HH_eso HH_ff)
          (precomp_ess_surj.pre_composition_essentially_surjective
             (C ⊠ C) (D ⊠ D) D Duniv HH HH_eso HH_ff))
       (TC ∙ H) (c1, c2))

      
C, D, E: category
H: C ⟶ D

C, D, E: category
H: C ⟶ D

Euniv: is_univalent E

TD:= TransportedTensor: D ⊠ D ⟶ D
G: [D, E]
HGG: functor_tensor_disp_cat TC TE
  (pre_composition_functor C D E H G)
Isos.is_z_iso_disp
  (identity_z_iso (pre_composition_functor C D E H G))
  ((λ c1 c2 : C,
    internal_paths_rew_r
      (E ⟦ TE (G (H c1), G (H c2)),
       G (H (TC (c1, c2))) ⟧)
      (lifted_functor_tensor HGG (H c1, H c2)
       · # G
           (rad_eps
              [precategory_binproduct_data D D, D]
              [precategory_binproduct_data C C, D]
              (pre_composition_functor (C ⊠ C) (D ⊠ D)
                 D HH)
              (ff_essentially_surjective_to_split
                 [precategory_binproduct_data D D, D]
                 [precategory_binproduct_data C C, D]
                 (is_univalent_functor_category
                    (precategory_binproduct_data D D)
                    D Duniv)
                 (pre_composition_functor (C ⊠ C)
                    (D ⊠ D) D HH)
                 (precomp_fully_faithful.pre_composition_with_ess_surj_and_fully_faithful_is_fully_faithful
                    (C ⊠ C) (D ⊠ D) D HH HH_eso HH_ff)
                 (precomp_ess_surj.pre_composition_essentially_surjective
                    (C ⊠ C) (D ⊠ D) D Duniv HH HH_eso
                    HH_ff)) (TC ∙ H) (c1, c2))
       · id G (H (TC (c1, c2))))
      (lifted_functor_tensor HGG (H c1, H c2)
       · # G
           (rad_eps
              [precategory_binproduct_data D D, D]
              [precategory_binproduct_data C C, D]
              (pre_composition_functor (C ⊠ C) (D ⊠ D)
                 D HH)
              (ff_essentially_surjective_to_split
                 [precategory_binproduct_data D D, D]
                 [precategory_binproduct_data C C, D]
                 (is_univalent_functor_category
                    (precategory_binproduct_data D D)
                    D Duniv)
                 (pre_composition_functor (C ⊠ C)
                    (D ⊠ D) D HH)
                 (precomp_fully_faithful.pre_composition_with_ess_surj_and_fully_faithful_is_fully_faithful
                    (C ⊠ C) (D ⊠ D) D HH HH_eso HH_ff)
                 (precomp_ess_surj.pre_composition_essentially_surjective
                    (C ⊠ C) (D ⊠ D) D Duniv HH HH_eso
                    HH_ff)) (TC ∙ H) (c1, c2)))
      (λ p : E ⟦ TE (G (H c1), G (H c2)),
             G (H (TC (c1, c2))) ⟧,
       # TE (id G (H c1) #, id G (H c2))
       · HGG (c1, c2) = p)
      (internal_paths_rew_r
         (E ⟦ TE (G (H c1), G (H c2)),
          TE (G (H c1), G (H c2)) ⟧)
         (# TE (id (G (H c1), G (H c2))))
         (id TE (G (H c1), G (H c2)))
         (λ p : E ⟦ TE (G (H c1), G (H c2)),

                     (D ⊠ D) D HH)

                     HH_ff)) (TC ∙ H) (c1, c2)))

        # TE (id G (H c1) #, id G (H c2))

                           HH_eso HH_ff)) (TC ∙ H)

                nat_trans_comp
                  (functor_tensor_map_dom TE
                     (functor_compose H G))

                     (functor_compose H G))

                     (nat_z_iso_inv
                        TransportedTensorComm) G)

       (ff_essentially_surjective_to_split
          [precategory_binproduct_data D D, D]
          [precategory_binproduct_data C C, D]
          (is_univalent_functor_category
             (precategory_binproduct_data D D) D Duniv)
          (pre_composition_functor (C ⊠ C) (D ⊠ D) D
             HH)
          (precomp_fully_faithful.pre_composition_with_ess_surj_and_fully_faithful_is_fully_faithful
             (C ⊠ C) (D ⊠ D) D HH HH_eso HH_ff)
          (precomp_ess_surj.pre_composition_essentially_surjective
             (C ⊠ C) (D ⊠ D) D Duniv HH HH_eso HH_ff))
       (TC ∙ H) (c1, c2)) = HGG (c1, c2)

H: C ⟶ D
Duniv: is_univalent D
Euniv: is_univalent E
H_eso: essentially_surjective H
H_ff: fully_faithful H
TC: C ⊠ C ⟶ C
TE: E ⊠ E ⟶ E

  (pre_composition_functor C D E H G)

  (functor_tensor_map_dom TE (functor_compose H G))

     G (c1, c2)

H_ff: fully_faithful H
TC: C ⊠ C ⟶ C
TE: E ⊠ E ⟶ E
HH_eso:= pair_functor_eso H H H_eso H_eso: essentially_surjective HH
HH_ff:= pair_functor_ff H H H_ff H_ff: fully_faithful HH
TD:= TransportedTensor: D ⊠ D ⟶ D
G1, G2: [D, E]
GG1: functor_tensor_disp_cat TD TE G1
GG2: functor_tensor_disp_cat TD TE G2
β: [D, E] ⟦ G1, G2 ⟧
y: HT G1 GG1 -->[
# (pre_composition_functor C D E H) β] 
HT G2 GG2
x, x': hfiber (λ ff : GG1 -->[ β] GG2, ♯ HT ff) y
isofhlevel 0 (x = x')

TD:= TransportedTensor: D ⊠ D ⟶ D
G1, G2: [D, E]
GG1: functor_tensor_disp_cat TD TE G1
GG2: functor_tensor_disp_cat TD TE G2
β: [D, E] ⟦ G1, G2 ⟧
y: HT G1 GG1 -->[
# (pre_composition_functor C D E H) β] 
HT G2 GG2

  (hfiber (λ ff : GG1 -->[ β] GG2, ♯ HT ff) y)
transportf
  (λ x : GG1 -->[ β] GG2,
   (λ ff : GG1 -->[ β] GG2, ♯ HT ff) x = y)
  (let X :=
     λ (TC : D ⊠ D ⟶ D) (TD : E ⊠ E ⟶ E) (F G : D ⟶ E)
     (FF : functor_tensor TC TD F)
     (GG : functor_tensor TC TD G) (α : F ⟹ G)
     (x x' : is_nat_trans_tensor TC TD FF GG α),
     pr1
       (isaprop_is_nat_trans_tensor TC TD FF GG α x x')
     in
   X TD TE G1 G2 GG1 GG2 β (pr1 x) (pr1 x')) (pr2 x) =
pr2 x'

C, D, E: category
H: C ⟶ D
Duniv: is_univalent D
Euniv: is_univalent E
H_eso: essentially_surjective H
H_ff: fully_faithful H
TC: C ⊠ C ⟶ C
TE: E ⊠ E ⟶ E
HH_eso:= pair_functor_eso H H H_eso H_eso: essentially_surjective HH
HH_ff:= pair_functor_ff H H H_ff H_ff: fully_faithful HH
TD:= TransportedTensor: D ⊠ D ⟶ D
G1, G2: [D, E]
GG1: functor_tensor_disp_cat TD TE G1
GG2: functor_tensor_disp_cat TD TE G2
β: [D, E] ⟦ G1, G2 ⟧
y: HT G1 GG1 -->[
# (pre_composition_functor C D E H) β] 
HT G2 GG2
x, x': hfiber (λ ff : GG1 -->[ β] GG2, ♯ HT ff) y
p: isaset
  (hfiber (λ ff : GG1 -->[ β] GG2, ♯ HT ff) y)
(λ cntr : x = x', ∏ t : x = x', t = cntr)
  (total2_paths_f
     (let X :=
        λ (TC : D ⊠ D ⟶ D) (TD : E ⊠ E ⟶ E)
        (F G : D ⟶ E) (FF : functor_tensor TC TD F)
        (GG : functor_tensor TC TD G) (α : F ⟹ G)
        (x x' : is_nat_trans_tensor TC TD FF GG α),
        pr1
          (isaprop_is_nat_trans_tensor TC TD FF GG α x
             x') in
      X TD TE G1 G2 GG1 GG2 β (pr1 x) (pr1 x'))
     (proofirrelevance
        ((λ ff : GG1 -->[ β] GG2, ♯ HT ff) (pr1 x') =
         y)
        (hlevelntosn 0
           ((λ ff : GG1 -->[ β] GG2, ♯ HT ff) (pr1 x') =
            y)
           (isaprop_is_nat_trans_tensor TC TE
              (HT G1 GG1) (HT G2 GG2)
              (# (pre_composition_functor C D E H) β)
              (♯ HT (pr1 x')) y))
        (transportf
           (λ x : GG1 -->[ β] GG2,
            (λ ff : GG1 -->[ β] GG2, ♯ HT ff) x = y)
           (let X :=
              λ (TC : D ⊠ D ⟶ D) (TD : E ⊠ E ⟶ E)
              (F G : D ⟶ E)
              (FF : functor_tensor TC TD F)
              (GG : functor_tensor TC TD G)
              (α : F ⟹ G)
              (x
               x' : is_nat_trans_tensor TC TD FF GG α),
              pr1
                (isaprop_is_nat_trans_tensor TC TD FF
                   GG α x x') in
            X TD TE G1 G2 GG1 GG2 β (pr1 x) (pr1 x'))
           (pr2 x)) (pr2 x')))
 intro ; apply p.
  Qed.

HH_eso:= pair_functor_eso H H H_eso H_eso: essentially_surjective HH

HT G2 GG2

C, D, E: category
H: C ⟶ D
Duniv: is_univalent D
Euniv: is_univalent E
H_eso: essentially_surjective H
H_ff: fully_faithful H
TC: C ⊠ C ⟶ C
TE: E ⊠ E ⟶ E
HH_eso:= pair_functor_eso H H H_eso H_eso: essentially_surjective HH
HH_ff:= pair_functor_ff H H H_ff H_ff: fully_faithful HH
TD:= TransportedTensor: D ⊠ D ⟶ D
G1, G2: [D, E]
GG1: functor_tensor_disp_cat TD TE G1
GG2: functor_tensor_disp_cat TD TE G2
β: [D, E] ⟦ G1, G2 ⟧
βHH: HT G1 GG1 -->[
# (pre_composition_functor C D E H) β] 
HT G2 GG2
cc: C ⊠ C
t:= βHH (pr1 cc) (pr2 cc): # TE
  (# (pre_composition_functor C D E H) β (pr1 cc)
  #, # (pre_composition_functor C D E H) β
       (pr2 cc)) · HT G2 GG2 (pr1 cc, pr2 cc) =
HT G1 GG1 (pr1 cc, pr2 cc)
· # (pre_composition_functor C D E H) β
    (TC (pr1 cc, pr2 cc))
ff:= # (pr1 G2)
  (pr1
     (pr2 TransportedTensorComm (pr1 cc, pr2 cc))): E
⟦ functor_tensor_map_codom TC
    (pre_composition_functor C D E H G2)
    (pr1 cc, pr2 cc),
functor_tensor_map_codom TD G2
  (H (pr1 cc), H (pr2 cc)) ⟧
p: pr1 GG2 (H (pr1 cc), H (pr2 cc)) =
pr1 (HT G2 GG2) (pr1 cc, pr2 cc) · ff
# TE (β (H (pr1 cc)) #, β (H (pr2 cc)))
· GG2 (H (pr1 cc), H (pr2 cc)) =
GG1 (H (pr1 cc), H (pr2 cc))
· β (TD (H (pr1 cc), H (pr2 cc)))

     (pr2 TransportedTensorComm (pr1 cc, pr2 cc))): E
⟦ functor_tensor_map_codom TC
    (pre_composition_functor C D E H G2)
    (pr1 cc, pr2 cc),
functor_tensor_map_codom TD G2
  (H (pr1 cc), H (pr2 cc)) ⟧
GG1 (H (pr1 cc), H (pr2 cc))
· (# G1
     (rad_eps [precategory_binproduct_data D D, D]
        [precategory_binproduct_data C C, D]
        (pre_composition_functor (C ⊠ C) (D ⊠ D) D HH)
        (ff_essentially_surjective_to_split
           [precategory_binproduct_data D D, D]
           [precategory_binproduct_data C C, D]
           (is_univalent_functor_category
              (precategory_binproduct_data D D) D
              Duniv)
           (pre_composition_functor (C ⊠ C) (D ⊠ D) D
              HH)
           (precomp_fully_faithful.pre_composition_with_ess_surj_and_fully_faithful_is_fully_faithful
              (C ⊠ C) (D ⊠ D) D HH HH_eso HH_ff)
           (precomp_ess_surj.pre_composition_essentially_surjective
              (C ⊠ C) (D ⊠ D) D Duniv HH HH_eso HH_ff))
        (TC ∙ H) (pr1 cc, pr2 cc))
   · (pr1 β (pr1 H (TC (pr1 cc, pr2 cc))) · ff)) =
GG1 (H (pr1 cc), H (pr2 cc))
· β (TD (H (pr1 cc), H (pr2 cc)))

           (precategory_binproduct_data D D) D Duniv)
        (pre_composition_functor (C ⊠ C) (D ⊠ D) D HH)
        (precomp_fully_faithful.pre_composition_with_ess_surj_and_fully_faithful_is_fully_faithful
           (C ⊠ C) (D ⊠ D) D HH HH_eso HH_ff)
        (precomp_ess_surj.pre_composition_essentially_surjective
           (C ⊠ C) (D ⊠ D) D Duniv HH HH_eso HH_ff))
     (TC ∙ H) (pr1 cc, pr2 cc))
· # G1
    (pr1 (pr2 TransportedTensorComm (pr1 cc, pr2 cc)))
· pr1 β ((HH ∙ TransportedTensor) (pr1 cc, pr2 cc)) =
β (TD (H (pr1 cc), H (pr2 cc)))
